<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositie</a> (25411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">composicie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">composition</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">composicion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">compositiō</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:componeren.html>componere</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to put together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The modern spelling <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">composition</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:composities.html>composities</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:compositie.html>compositietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>The composition (general) makeup of something, notably in <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> of components such as ingredients; especially a (metallic) alloy</li>
<li>A musical composition, piece written by a composer</li>
<li>An artistic composition, arrangement as of figures in a scene, colors on a canvas etc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">treaty</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">contract</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">settlement</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:compressie.html>compressie</a> (54795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">compression</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">compressio</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:computervirus.html>computervirus</a> (43957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">computer</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">virus</i>
</p>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:computervirus.html>computervirus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:computervirussen.html>computervirussen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:computervirus.html>computervirusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:concentratie.html>concentratie</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kamp.html>kamp</a></i>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">concentration camp</i>. Attested since the late nineteenth century (see citation page).

***concertina.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a> (94485)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">concertinas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A musical instrument, like the various accordions, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a member of the free-reed family of musical instruments, typically having <a href = vnd.unilang:buttons.html>buttons</a> on both <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1913</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_C._Lincoln" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Joseph C. Lincoln">Joseph C. Lincoln</a>,  chapter 8, in  <cite><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://openlibrary.org/works/OL5535161W"><a href = vnd.unilang:mr.html>Mr</a>. Pratt's Patients</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">That <b><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a wonder in its way. The handles that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> on it first <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> wore out long ago, and he'd made new <a href = vnd.unilang:ones.html>ones</a> of braided rope yarn. And the <a href = vnd.unilang:bellows.html>bellows</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> patched in more <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a> than a cranberry <a href = vnd.unilang:picker.html>picker</a>'s <a href = vnd.unilang:overalls.html>overalls</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>Something resembling a <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a>, such as a folded book, a <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>bus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> or a set of picture <a href = vnd.unilang:frames.html>frames</a> that are folded together.</li>
<li>Coiled barbed wire for use as an obstacle.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup></li>
<li>A type of booklet label, consisting of up to 32 pages of booklet as an insert.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">concertinist</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a> book</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a> frame</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">concertinas</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">concertinaing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">concertinaed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to become compressed into a shape reminiscent of a <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a>
<dl><dd><i>The car <b>concertinaed</b> into the wall.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:amy.html>Amy</a> Schoeman, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Skeleton_Coast" class="extiw" title="w:Skeleton Coast">Skeleton Coast</a></i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ru/books?id=W75aoZLDG9YCamp;lpg=RA1-PR2amp;dq=concertinaedamp;pg=RA1-PR2v=onepageamp;q=concertinaedamp;f=false">page ii</a>
<dl><dd>Millions of years ago the <a href = vnd.unilang:mica.html>mica</a> schists surrounding the old Brandberg West Mine became folded and <b>concertinaed</b> by enormous horizontal pressures.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>to be drawn <a href = vnd.unilang:closer.html>closer</a> and farther apart repeatedly, or up and down, as if situated on a working <a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a>'s folds
<ul><li><b>2007</b>, David W Cameron, <i>25 April 1915: The Day the Anzac Legend <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> Born</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ru/books?id=XyxIQIg0TPcCamp;lpg=PA36amp;dq=concertinaedamp;pg=PA36v=onepageamp;q=concertinaedamp;f=false">page 36</a>
<dl><dd>This resulted in some fragmentation of the line as the <a href = vnd.unilang:boats.html>boats</a> in some <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> closed to just 50 metres as they <b>concertinaed</b> in and out of sight of each other.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:concertina.html>concertina</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:muziekinstrument.html>muziekinstrument</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> trekzak gelijkende <a href = vnd.unilang:kleine.html>kleine</a>, zeshoekige <a href = vnd.unilang:accordeon.html>accordeon</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">conclave</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">conclave</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">conclāve</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">room that may be locked up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">con-</i> (combining form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cum</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clāvis</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">key</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).

***conclusie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:conclusie.html>conclusie</a> (5828)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:conclusie.html>conclusie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">conclusion</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">conclūsiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:conclusie.html>conclusie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:conclusies.html>conclusies</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:conclusie.html>conclusietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>conclusion</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">European Union law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> opinion (judicial opinion delivered by an Advocate General to the European Court of Justice for a legal solution in a case)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:condens.html>condens</a> (94480)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">condom</i>, either named for a British physician (during Charles II's reign) or from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">guantone</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">guanto</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">glove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kondom</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">condom</i>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:confectie.html>confectie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>

***confederatie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:confederatie.html>confederatie</a> (21676)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnfoederātiō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:confederatie.html>confederatie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:confederatie.html>confederaties</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:confederatie.html>confederatietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a confederation; an union or alliance of (largely) independent sovereign states or political organizations
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">statenbond</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms coordinate-term"><span class="defdate">Coordinate <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a>:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bondsstaat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">eenheidsstaat</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:federatie.html>federatie</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>In Belgian politics, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used by some parties to describe a federation where most decision power rests with the regional governments and parliaments.
</p>

***confessor.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:confessor.html>confessor</a> (13853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:confessor.html>confessor</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">confessour</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anglo-Norman_language" class="extiw" title="w:Anglo-Norman language">Anglo-Norman</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">confessour</i>, and its source, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnfessor</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cōnfiteor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confess, admit, acknowledge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:confessor.html>confessor</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:confessors.html>confessors</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="en">confessoress</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One who confesses faith in Christianity in the face of persecution, but who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not martyred.
<ul><li><b>2009</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Diarmaid_MacCulloch" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Diarmaid MacCulloch">Diarmaid MacCulloch</a>, <i>A History of Christianity</i>, Penguin 2010, p. 174:
<dl><dd><b><a href = vnd.unilang:confessors.html>Confessors</a></b> provided the troubled Church with an alternative sort of authority based on their sufferings, particularly when arguments began about how and how much to forgive those Christians who <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> given way to imperial <a href = vnd.unilang:orders.html>orders</a> – the so-called ‘lapsed’.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>One who confesses to having done something wrong.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Roman Catholicism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A priest who hears confession and then gives absolution</li></ol>
</body>

***confetti.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a> (29391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed (possibly <a href = vnd.unilang:via.html>via</a> French) from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">confections</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, used to describe sugar-coated almonds, and by extension <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> imitating them (like pellets of plaster), which <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> thrown in Italy during festivities like Carnival and weddings.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Spread_of_Confetti_2-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Spread_of_Confetti-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> (This practice <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> mentioned in English since at least the 1810s.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>) The French and the English adopted the practice of celebrating weddings and other festivities by throwing such candies, or (by the late 1800s) tiny pieces of colored paper symbolizing them,<sup id="cite_ref-ODWO_5-0" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-ODWO-5"> | 5 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-6"> | 6 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-7"> | 7 | </a></sup> partially displacing their earlier practice of throwing rice.<sup id="cite_ref-Spread_of_Confetti_2-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-Spread_of_Confetti-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a></strong> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Small pieces or <a href = vnd.unilang:strips.html>strips</a> (streamers) of colored paper or other material (metal, plaster, etc) generally thrown about at festive <a href = vnd.unilang:occasions.html>occasions</a>, especially at weddings and in victory celebrations.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Edible Italian sugar-coated almonds, especially those which are used as part of a traditional Italian wedding.
<ul><li><b>1870</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>. Tuckerman, in the <i>Boston Transcript</i>, quoted in <i>The New York Observer Yearbook and Almanac</i>, page 143:
<dl><dd>[...] a pale and fair devotee of fashion who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> left off eating <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a></b></i>, and recovered her bloom.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1959</b>, Loren Wahl, Lorenzo Madalena, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>Confetti</a> for <a href = vnd.unilang:gino.html>Gino</a></i>:
<dl><dd>"Why, if you and Teresa, our own <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> and maid of honor . . . <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>oh</a>, how wonderful that would be, to eat <b><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a></b> at your wedding!"</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1975</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:garibaldi.html>Garibaldi</a> Marto Lapolla, <i>The grand Gennaro</i>, Ayer Co. Pub.:
<dl><dd>Emilio and Roberto <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> pooled their resources in money and <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> arranged with the cafe keeper for steaming thick chocolate, a slow-pouring syrup-like <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a>, the richest <i>boccotoni</i>, cream-filled heavy <i>sfogliate</i>, and almond <b><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1986</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:anne.html>Anne</a> Paolucci, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:sepia.html>Sepia</a> tones: seven short <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>stories</a></i>, Council on Natl Literature (→ISBN):
<dl><dd>There <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> large trays with assorted pastries and colored almond <b><a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a></b> for a wedding, and he remembered with a <a href = vnd.unilang:pang.html>pang</a> that this very day <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> the wedding anniversary, the day <a href = vnd.unilang:pino.html>Pino</a> and <a href = vnd.unilang:maria.html>Maria</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> married (so long ago!) in <a href = vnd.unilang:rome.html>Rome</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="see-cites">For more examples of usage of this term, see Citations:<a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a>.</span></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Very rarely, a single piece of <a href = vnd.unilang:confetti.html>confetti</a> may be called a <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">confetto</i>, as in Italian.</li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:confrater.html>confrater</a> (132375)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:confrater.html>confrater</a></i>, from com- (a form of con-) 'together' + <a href = vnd.unilang:frater.html>frater</a> 'brother, fellow'. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">confrere</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Mitbruder</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A confrere, professional colleague, notably in an esteemed, learned profession, especially lawyer</li>
<li>A fellow member, as of a confraternity</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A confrere, comrade, cahoot</li></ol>

***confronteren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:confronteren.html>confronteren</a> (12178)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">confronter</i>.

***congres.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:congres.html>congres</a> (4076)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">congressum</i>, the past participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">congredi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go or come together</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">con-</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">gradi</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go or step</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:congres.html>congres</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:congressen.html>congressen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:congres.html>congresje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>congress, large consultative and/or legislative body</li>
<li>congress; formal meeting, gathering or assembly</li></ol>

***congreszaal.html
